}</pre>\\n108:  *\\n109:  * This instance can also be used to pass in custom configurations to different modules (e.g. passing a special config in your customized serde class).\\n110:  * The consumer/producer/admin prefix can also be used to distinguish these custom config values passed to different clients with the same config name.\\n111:  * * Example:\\n112:  * <pre>{@code\\n113:  * streamsProperties.put(StreamsConfig.producerPrefix(\\\"my.custom.config\\\"), \\\"bar\\\");\\n118:  * // sets \\\"my.custom.config2\\\" to \\\"boom\\\" for all clients universally\\n119:  * streamsProperties.put(\\\"my.custom.config2\\\", \\\"boom\\\");\\n120:  *\\n121:  * // as a result, inside producer's serde class configure(..) function,\\n122:  * // users can now read both key-value group ID</li>\\n144:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#ENABLE_AUTO_COMMIT_CONFIG \\\"enable.auto.commit\\\"} (false) - Streams client will always disable/turn off auto committing</li>\\n145:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#PARTITION_ASSIGNMENT_STRATEGY_CONFIG \\\"partition.assignment.strategy\\\"} (<code>StreamsPartitionAssignor</code>) - Streams client will always use its own partition you should prefix those properties using\n89:  * {@link #consumerPrefix(String)}, {@link #producerPrefix(String)} and {@link #adminClientPrefix(String)}, respectively.\n90:  * <p>\n91:  * Example:\n92:  * <pre>{@code\n93:  * // potentially wrong: sets \"metadata.max.age.ms\" to 1 minute for producer AND consumer\n94:  * Properties streamsProperties = new Properties();\n95:  * streamsProperties.put(StreamsConfig.producerPrefix(ProducerConfig.METADATA_MAX_AGE_CONFIG), 60000);\n105:  *\n106:  * StreamsConfig streamsConfig = new StreamsConfig(streamsProperties);\n107:  * }</pre>\n108:  *\n109:  * This instance can also be used to pass in custom configurations to different modules (e.g. passing a special config in your customized serde class).\n110:  * The consumer/producer/admin prefix can also be used to distinguish these custom config values passed to different clients with the same config name.\n111:  * * Example:\n112:  * <pre>{@code\n113:  * \"foo\");\n116:  * // sets \"my.custom.config\" to \"bar\" for producer only\n117:  * streamsProperties.put(StreamsConfig.producerPrefix(\"my.custom.config\"), \"bar\");\n118:  * // sets \"my.custom.config2\" to \"boom\" for all clients universally\n119:  * streamsProperties.put(\"my.custom.config2\", \"boom\");\n120:  *\n121:  * // as a result, inside producer's serde class configure(..) function,\n122:  * // users can now read both key-value pairs \"my.custom.config\" -> \"foo\"\n123:  * // and \"my.custom.config2\" -> \"boom\" from the config map\n124:  * StreamsConfig streamsConfig = new StreamsConfig(streamsProperties);\n125:  * }</pre>\n126:  *\n127:  *\n128:  * When increasing {@link ProducerConfig#MAX_BLOCK_MS_CONFIG} to be more resilient to non-available </pre>\n133:  *\n134:  *\n135:  * Kafka Streams requires at least the following properties to be set:\n136:  * <ul>\n137:  *  <li>{@link #APPLICATION_ID_CONFIG \"application.id\"}</li>\n138:  *  <li>{@link #BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS_CONFIG \"bootstrap.servers\"}</li>\n139:  * </ul>\n140:  *\n141:  * By default, Kafka Streams does not allow users to overwrite the following properties (Streams setting shown in parentheses):\n142:  * <ul>\n143:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#GROUP_ID_CONFIG \"group.id\"} (&lt;application.id&gt;) - Streams client will always use the application ID a consumer group ID</li>\n144:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#ENABLE_AUTO_COMMIT_CONFIG \"enable.auto.commit\"} (false) - Streams client will always disable/turn off auto committing</li>\n145:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#PARTITION_ASSIGNMENT_STRATEGY_CONFIG \"partition.assignment.strategy\"} (<code>StreamsPartitionAssignor</code>) - Streams client will always use its own partition assignor</li>\n146:  * </ul>\n147:  *\n148:  * If {@link #PROCESSING_GUARANTEE_CONFIG \"processing.guarantee\"} is set to {@link #EXACTLY_ONCE_V2 \"exactly_once_v2\"},\n149:  * Kafka Streams does not allow users to
